=== Question 1 (ID: Mercury_417466) ===
Q: Which statement best explains why photosynthesis is the foundation of most food webs?
Choices:
  *(A) Sunlight is the source of energy for nearly all ecosystems.
   (B) Most ecosystems are found on land instead of in water.
   (C) Carbon dioxide is more available than other gases.
   (D) The producers in all ecosystems are plants.
Answer: (A) Sunlight is the source of energy for nearly all ecosystems.

=== Question 2 (ID: Mercury_7081673) ===
Q: Which piece of safety equipment is used to keep mold spores from entering the respiratory system?
Choices:
   (A) safety goggles
  *(B) breathing mask
   (C) rubber gloves
   (D) lead apron
Answer: (B) breathing mask

=== Question 5 (ID: Mercury_7037258) ===
Q: Which best describes the structure of an atom?
Choices:

  *(B) a massive core surrounded by negatively-charged particles
   (C) a network of interacting positive and negative particles

=== Question 10 (ID: Mercury_SC_413631) ===
Q: Which of these correctly identifies the way materials are transported in a plant?
Choices:
  *(A) Xylem carries water from the roots to the leaves.
   (B) Phloem carries minerals from the roots to the leaves.
   (C) Xylem carries sugars from the flowers to the stems.
   (D) Phloem carries water from the flowers to the stems.
Answer: (A) Xylem carries water from the roots to the leaves.
